  474. I have eczema and have had delicate, sensitive skin since forever, and I finally got fed up with this latest flare-up. It's covering my hands and creeping up my arms. I'm scientifically trained and work at a university, so I hopped on PubMed to look at what factors influence how well skin retains moisture. One of the only products that looked like it had potential was hyaluronic acid. It's a humectant, so it helps your skin draw moisture from the air. (Lots of my other favorite active ingredients, like dimethicone, create a barrier that prevents moisture from escaping, since your skin's mechanisms that are supposed to keep the water inside are failing, but humectants work differently.) I got a bottle of this figuring it was only fifteen bucks if it didn't work and if it did, great. A difference doesn't need to be dramatic for me to appreciate it--it can be the difference between staying up all night scratching my arms and being able to sleep. I've gotten in the habit of rubbing a couple of drops into my hands before moisturizing after I wash my hands. (I layer it in that order because my moisturizer of choice has dimethicone and heavier ingredients like that can prevent lighter ingredients from getting to the skin.) I use it at home, and I don't use it at work, and almost immediately I noticed that on weekends when I'm at home all day my hands start doing better than when I'm at work. It's not a miracle, but it's an improvement. At this point I'm contemplating getting the big bottle for home and using the smaller bottle at work. I also use it on my face, particularly on my fine lines and wrinkles; it's definitely not causing me any break-outs and I like the way it feels on my skin. It also seems to help provide a calming balance to retinol-based creams (though I had to give those up when I got an eczema outbreak around my eyes).

I see subtle differences in my skin tone, but not my pores, wrinkles, or tightness of skin. I believe this serum could be used for everyday maintenance, aging prevention in skin, and overall brightness and clarity. But if you're looking to reverse skin aging, wrinkles, or loose skin then you'll need to mix this serum in with another cream that does the trick. Think of this as a booster to your existing skincare routine.

So it is difficult for me to find that good balance where the oily spots are cleaned up and the dry spots are not dried out more. So I've been testing each of the hyaluronic acids on a different spot of my face or hands where I have dryness issues. I also have fairly sensitive skin, and my review also includes how well the product does without irritating my skin.<br /><br />This particular hyaluronic acid serum was tested on my forehead between my brows, where I often fight with dry, flaky skin.<br /><br />Hydration - As far as hydration goes, the product did well. I did see a noticeable difference in the &#34;flakiness&#34; of my skin between my brows.<br /><br />Sensitivity - Unlike another product I had tried in the same area, this one did well to not irritate my skin. I did not notice any redness or itching after using the serum.<br /><br />Application - The product was easy to apply. It comes with an eye-dropper cap. I just put a drop or two on the tips of my fingers and massaged it in. I didn't apply directly to my forehead because I didn't want it running down my nose. You don't have to use a lot of the product, and you can target just the areas that need hydration.<br /><br />Feel of product - I am generally not a fan of skincare products as I can always feel them lying on my skin. I don't like that sticky, heavy feeling that some products (especially sunblock) leave on your skin. This serum did not leave me feeling sticky or uncomfortable. It absorbed quickly and had no weighty feel.<br /><br />Based on those categories, I think this product is a good hyaluronic acid serum. And top it off with the fact that it is made in the USA, I do recommend it for your skin dryness issues.

I gave this Hyaluronic Acid Serum 100% Pure (2oz/60ml) Cosmedica Skincare- Intense Hydration + Moisture, Non-greasy, Paraben-free (Professional Formula) Sold by Cosmedica Skincare only 2 stars because it is not what the name of it implies.
